/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [GetNotificationDetail]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
DROP PROCEDURE [GetNotificationDetail]
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [GetNotificationDetail]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [GetNotificationDetail]
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	SELECT Announcement, NotifiedOn, DeviceType,  COUNT(1) AS NotificationCount FROM
	(SELECT P.PageHeaderText AS Announcement, CAST(N.NotifiedOn AS DATE) AS NotifiedOn, 
	CASE WHEN D.DeviceType = 1 THEN 'Android' ELSE 'iOS' END AS DeviceType
	FROM NotificationLog N WITH (NOLOCK)
	INNER JOIN DeviceRegistry D WITH (NOLOCK) ON D.DeviceRegistryId = N.DeviceRegistryId AND D.StatusId = 1
	INNER JOIN PageItem P WITH (NOLOCK) ON P.PageItemId = N.PageItemId AND P.StatusId = 1
	WHERE N.StatusId = 1)TBL1
	GROUP BY Announcement, NotifiedOn, DeviceType
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [InsertNotificationLog]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [InsertNotificationLog]
(
	@NotifiactionToken VARCHAR(200),
	@DeviceId VARCHAR(200),
	@PageItemId INT
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @trancount int;
	SET @trancount = @@trancount;
	BEGIN TRY
		IF @trancount = 0
			BEGIN TRANSACTION
		ELSE
			SAVE TRANSACTION InsertNotificationLog;

		IF EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM DeviceRegistry WHERE DeviceId = @DeviceId AND StatusId = 1)
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @DeviceRegistryId AS INT;
			SELECT @DeviceRegistryId = DeviceRegistryId FROM DeviceRegistry WHERE DeviceId = @DeviceId AND StatusId = 1

			INSERT INTO NotificationLog(NotifiactionToken,DeviceRegistryId,PageItemId,StatusId,IsRead,NotifiedOn)
			VALUES(@NotifiactionToken,@DeviceRegistryId,@PageItemId,1,0,GETDATE());

			SELECT @@IDENTITY AS NotificationLogId;
		END

	LBEXIT:
		IF @trancount = 0	
			COMMIT;
	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		DECLARE @error INT, @message VARCHAR(4000), @xstate INT;
		SELECT @error = ERROR_NUMBER(), @message = ERROR_MESSAGE(), @xstate = XACT_STATE();
		IF @xstate = -1
			ROLLBACK;
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount = 0
			ROLLBACK
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount > 0
			ROLLBACK TRANSACTION InsertNotificationLog;

		RAISERROR ('InsertNotificationLog: %d: %s', 16, 1, @error, @message) ;
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [InsertPageItem]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [InsertPageItem]
(
	@PageId INT,
	@PageItemType INT = 100,
	@PageHeaderText VARCHAR(1000),
	@PageSubHeaderText VARCHAR(1000),
	@PageItemImage VARCHAR(200),
	@PageItemDetailText VARCHAR(MAX),
	@PageItemSubDetail VARCHAR(1000),
	@StatusId INT,
	@CreatedOn DATETIME,
	@ActivatedOn DATETIME,
	@ItemOrder INT
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @trancount int;
	SET @trancount = @@trancount;
	BEGIN TRY
		IF @trancount = 0
			BEGIN TRANSACTION
		ELSE
			SAVE TRANSACTION InsertPageItem;

		DECLARE @PageItemId INT
		SET @CreatedOn = GETDATE();
		SET @ActivatedOn = GETDATE();
		
		SELECT @PageItemId = COALESCE(MAX(PageItemId), (@PageId * 1000)) + 1 FROM PageItem WHERE PageId = @PageId

		IF EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM PageItem WHERE PageItemId = @PageItemId)
		BEGIN
			SELECT @PageItemId = COALESCE(MAX(PageItemId), 0) + 1 FROM PageItem
		END

		INSERT INTO PageItem(PageItemId,PageId,PageItemType,PageHeaderText,PageSubHeaderText,
			PageItemImage,PageItemDetailText,PageItemSubDetail,StatusId,CreatedOn,ActivatedOn,ItemOrder)
		VALUES(@PageItemId,@PageId,@PageItemType,@PageHeaderText,@PageSubHeaderText,
			@PageItemImage,@PageItemDetailText,@PageItemSubDetail,@StatusId,@CreatedOn,@ActivatedOn,@ItemOrder)

		SELECT PageItemId,PageId,PageItemType,PageHeaderText,PageSubHeaderText,PageItemImage,PageItemDetailText,
		PageItemSubDetail,StatusId,CreatedOn,ActivatedOn,UpdatedOn,Version,ItemOrder FROM PageItem WHERE PageItemId = @PageItemId

	LBEXIT:
		IF @trancount = 0	
			COMMIT;
	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		DECLARE @error INT, @message VARCHAR(4000), @xstate INT;
		SELECT @error = ERROR_NUMBER(), @message = ERROR_MESSAGE(), @xstate = XACT_STATE();
		IF @xstate = -1
			ROLLBACK;
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount = 0
			ROLLBACK
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount > 0
			ROLLBACK TRANSACTION InsertPageItem;

		RAISERROR ('InsertPageItem: %d: %s', 16, 1, @error, @message) ;
	END CATCH
END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [MarkReadNotificationLog]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [MarkReadNotificationLog]
(
	@NotifiactionToken VARCHAR(200),
	@DeviceId VARCHAR(200)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @trancount int;
	SET @trancount = @@trancount;
	BEGIN TRY
		IF @trancount = 0
			BEGIN TRANSACTION
		ELSE
			SAVE TRANSACTION MarkReadNotificationLog;


		IF (EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM DeviceRegistry WHERE DeviceId = @DeviceId AND StatusId = 1) AND
		EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM NotificationLog WHERE NotifiactionToken = @NotifiactionToken AND StatusId = 1))
		BEGIN
			UPDATE N SET N.ReadOn = GETDATE(), N.IsRead = 1 FROM NotificationLog N
			INNER JOIN DeviceRegistry D ON N.DeviceRegistryId = D.DeviceRegistryId
			WHERE DeviceId = @DeviceId AND NotifiactionToken = @NotifiactionToken 
			AND N.StatusId = 1 AND D.StatusId = 1
			
			SELECT 1 AS NotificationRead;
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			SELECT 0 AS NotificationRead;
		END

	LBEXIT:
		IF @trancount = 0	
			COMMIT;
	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		DECLARE @error INT, @message VARCHAR(4000), @xstate INT;
		SELECT @error = ERROR_NUMBER(), @message = ERROR_MESSAGE(), @xstate = XACT_STATE();
		IF @xstate = -1
			ROLLBACK;
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount = 0
			ROLLBACK
		IF @xstate = 1 and @trancount > 0
			ROLLBACK TRANSACTION MarkReadNotificationLog;

		RAISERROR ('MarkReadNotificationLog: %d: %s', 16, 1, @error, @message) ;
	END CATCH
END

GO

/****** Object:  View [HitCounterDetail]    Script Date: 7/12/2015 11:14:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [HitCounterDetail]
AS
SELECT SponsorType = CASE WHEN HC.SponsorTypeId = 2 THEN 'Banner' ELSE 'Splash' END,
COALESCE(B.BannerName, S.SplashName) AS Name,
COALESCE(B.ImageUrl, S.ImageUrl) AS ImageUrl,
COALESCE(B.SponsorUrl, S.SponsorUrl) AS SponsorUrl,
HC.ClientIdentiy AS ClientIdentity, ISNULL(HC.HitOn, GETDATE()) AS HitOn FROM HitCounter HC
LEFT OUTER JOIN BannerItem B ON HC.SponsorId = B.BannerItemId AND HC.SponsorTypeId = 2 AND B.StatusId = 1
LEFT OUTER JOIN SplashImage S ON HC.SponsorId = S.SplashImageId AND HC.SponsorTypeId = 1 AND S.StatusId = 1
WHERE (B.BannerItemId IS NOT NULL OR S.SplashImageId IS NOT NULL) AND HC.StatusId = 1
GO
